 vah shiksha mantri bhi rahi thim

 tippaniyan Lord Bell told Sky News Channel, "we will never see leaders like him
 vah england ke sarvshereshth pradhanmantriyon main se ek thim
 "he described Thatcher as the greatest leader of the Conservative Party other than Winston Churchill
 thatcher ko ek roosi patrkaar ne 1976 main rus ke samyawad kaa virodh karne par 'aayran ladi' kaa sambodhan diya tha
 On Thatcher's death, Prime Minister Manmohan Singh expressed his convictions and said that under Thatcher's leadership, England had achieved significant progress at the national and international level
 apane shok sandesh main manmohan singh ne kaha, "main england kii purv pradhanmantri baroness margrat thatcher ke nidhan par apni gahari samvedanaaen vyakt karata hum
 " england ke pradhanmantri david camran ne duniya ke kai raajnneetigyon ke saath thatcher ko bhaavbheene shradhanjali arpit kii
 Cameron said, "I am deeply saddened to learn of Thatcher's death
 hamane ek mahaan netaa, ek mahaan pradhanmantri or ek mahaan englandwasi ko kho diya he
 " thatcher ke nidhan kaa samachar milane par england kii maharani elizabeth bhi kaaphi dukhi ho gayi
 a statement issued from Buckingham Palace stated, "queen Elizabeth Baroness was saddened to hear the news of Thatcher's demise
 maharani, thatcher ke parivaar ko sahanubhuti sandesh bhejengi
 " america raashtrapati ronaald reagan ke atirikt thatcher apni samakaleen bhartiya pradhanmantri indira gandhi ke bhi kaaphi najadik thim
 Thatcher was also a clear admirer of Indira Gandhi, known for her equally harsh decisions
 1995 main apni bharat yatra ko dauraan thatcher ne kaha tha, "hamaare bich bahut jaldi hi achche sambandh sthapit ho gaye, ham donon hi sarvocch karyaalayon kii ekantata kaa anubhav karte hai or kisi aise vyakti se baat karnaa acha lagata he jo aapako samajhataa ho
 " indira gandhi ke bare main thatcher ne kaha tha, "lekin maine unamem aisi yogyataayen dekhin jo meri samaj se ek raajnneetijna ke liye aavashyak hai
 He was proud of his country to the extent of his passion
 vah hameshaa nirbhay rahati thim or bahut hi vyaavhaarik thim
 " 1984 main irish ganraajya kii sena dwaara briton hotel par conservative party kii baithak ke dauraan kiye gaye hamale main bal-bal bachane ke baad thatcher ko sabase pehle jin kuch chuninda logon ne sandesh bheje the, unamem se indira gandhi bhi thim
 According to England news channel Sky News, Thatcher was admitted to the hospital just before Christmas where her kidney was operated upon
 navvarsh se pehle vah aspataal se ghar aa gai thim
 Thatcher, the leader of the Conservative Party, was the Prime Minister of Britain from 1979 to 1990, and withdrew from public life due to ill health
 unki sarkaar ne kai sarkari udyogon kaa nijeekaran kiya
 Born in 1925, Margaret Roberts was elected to the House of Commons, the lower house of the British Parliament, for the first time on the Conservative Party ticket in 1959
 varsh 1992 main unhone raajnneeti se sanyas le liya
 He won the general elections in the years 1979, 1983 and 1987
 vah shiksha mantri bhi rahi thim
 Thatcher is credited with making England the world's leading industrialized country
 tippaniyan Lord Bell told Sky News Channel, "we will never see leaders like him
 vah england ke sarvshereshth pradhanmantriyon main se ek thim
 "he described Thatcher as the greatest leader of the Conservative Party other than Winston Churchill
 thatcher ko ek roosi patrkaar ne 1976 main rus ke samyawad kaa virodh karne par 'aayran ladi' kaa sambodhan diya tha
 In his condolence message, Manmohan Singh said, "I express my deepest condolences on the demise of former England Prime Minister Baroness Margaret Thatcher
 " The Prime Minister of England, David Cameron, along with many politicians of the world paid a warm tribute to Thatcher
 camran ne kaha, "thatcher ke nidhan ke bare main jaanakar mujhe behad dukh hua he
 We have lost a great leader, a great Prime Minister and a great Englishman
 " Queen Elizabeth of England also became very sad when news of Thatcher died
 buckingham pales se jari ek vaktavy main kaha gaya he, "maharani elizabeth baroness thatcher ke nidhan kaa samachar sunakar dukhi ho gayi
 The Queen will send a sympathy message to Thatcher's family
 " Apart from US President Ronald Reagan, Thatcher was also very close to her contemporary Indian Prime Minister Indira Gandhi
 thatcher apane hi samaan kathor faislon ke liye jaani jane vaali indira gandhi kii spasht prashansak bhi thim
 During his visit to India in 1995, Thatcher said, "we have established very good relations very soon, we both feel the seclusion of the highest offices and it is nice to talk to someone who understands you
 " Regarding Indira Gandhi, Thatcher said, "but i saw in him the qualifications that i think are necessary for a politician
" unhen apane desh par junun kii had tak garv tha
 She was always fearless and very practical
 " Indira Gandhi was one of the first few who sent messages to Thatcher after narrowly escaping an attack on the Briton Hotel by the Irish Republic army in 1984 during a Conservative Party meeting
 england ke samachar channel ski news ke anusaar thatcher ko christmas se thik pehle aspataal main bhartee karaayaa gaya tha jahaan unke gurde kaa aaparishan kiya gaya
 She had come home from the hospital before New Year
 kanjarvative party kii netaa thatcher varsh 1979 se 1990 ke bich britain kii pradhanmantri thim or kharaab swasthya ke kaaran saarvajanik jivan se dur ho gai thim
 His government privatized many government industries
 1925 main janmi margrat roberts varsh 1959 main kanjarvative party ke tikat par pehali baar british sansad ke nimna sadan house of comons ke liye nirvaachit hui thim
 In the year 1992, he retired from politics
 unhone varsh 1979, 1983 or 1987 main aam chunaav jeeta tha
 She had also been the Minister of Education
 thatcher ko england ko duniya kaa agrani audyogic desh banane kaa shrey jaataa he
 The comments lord bel ne ski news channel se kaha, "unke jaisi netaa hamen kabhi dikhaai nahin dengi
 She was one of the best prime ministers of England
 " unhone thatcher ko winston churchill ke atirikt kanjarvative party kaa sabase mahaan netaa bataaya

 The western Uttar Pradesh bandh called by the Bharatiya Janata Party (BJP) on Sunday had a mixed effect
 mujffarnagar sahit rajya ke pashchimi hisse ke kareeb 15 jilon main pramukh bazaar or vyavsaayik pratishthan band rahe
 Shops remained open in areas with mixed populations
 band ke maddenjar suraksha ke kade intjaam kiye gaye the
 During this time there is no news of violence from anywhere
 bhaajapa kii uttar pradesh ikai ne mujffarnagar hinsa ke sambandh main apane do vidhayakon kii giraftaar ke virodh main ravivaar ko pashchimi uttar pradesh band kaa aahvaan kiya tha
 The party announced a sit-in demonstration across the state on Monday
 meerut, mujffarnagar, saharanpur, gajiabad, bulandshahr, shamali, hapur, bagpat, bijanour, muradabad sahit pashchimi uttar pradesh ke kareeb 15 jilon main pramukh bazaaron main subah se sannata pasra rahaa, haalanki mishrit aabaadi vaale ilaakon main dukaane khuli raheen
 There was movement of people on the streets
 mujffarnagar shahar main bhagat singh road, esady market, molahedi bazaar, daal mandi sahit adhiktar pramukh bazaar band rahe
 Shops remained open in Muslim dominated areas
 vahiin meerut main subah se bhaajapa kaaryakarta pradesh adhyaksh lakshmikaat vaajapeyi kii aguwai main vyapaariyon se dukaane band karne kaa aagrah karte najar aae
 bjp's bandh got the support of businessmen
 adhiktar bazaaron main dinabhar taale latake rahe
 BJP state spokesperson Vijay Bahudar Pathak said that a peaceful bandh was called in western Uttar Pradesh on Sunday to protest against the discriminatory and unilateral action of the state government
 meerut sahit pashchimi uttar pradesh ke vibhinn shaharon ke vyapaariyon ne band main bhaajapa ko puraa sahyog kiya
 The bandh was not only unprecedented, but received effective public support
 unhone samaajawaadee party (sapa) sarkaar par aarope lagaate hue kaha ki bijanour sahit kuch jilon main police ne jiladhyakshon ko shanivaar ko hi hiraasat main le liya tha
 In such a situation, the bandh called by the party was completely successful
 vahiin prashasan kii taraf se kaha gaya tha ki agar bhaajapa kaaryakartaaon ne kahin par jabaran dukaane band karaane kii koshish kii to unke khilaaf karrwai hogi haalanki meerut, noida, saharanpur, rampur jaise kuch sthanon par bhaajapa kaaryakartaaon dwaara jabaran dukaane band karwaane kii khabaren ain
 The comments ullekhneey he ki police ne mujffarnagar hinsa ke aarope main do bhaajapa vidhayakon- sangeet som or suresh rana- ko giraftaar kiya he
 Pathak told that there will be a sit-in demonstration on Monday at all the district headquarters of the state to protest against the arrest of BJP mlas and the unilateral action of the SP government
 jiske jariye bhaajapa netaa or kaaryakarta pradesh sarkaar ke ek paksheeya ravaie ko janata ke samaksh rakhenge
 The Uttar Pradesh unit of the BJP on Sunday called for a western Uttar Pradesh bandh in protest against the arrest of two of its mlas in connection with the Muzaffarnagar violence
 party ne somvaar ko pradeshbhar main dharna-pradarshnaki ghoshnaa kii he
 Around 15 districts of western Uttar Pradesh, including Meerut, Muzaffarnagar, Saharanpur, Ghaziabad, Bulandshahr, Shamli, Hapur, Baghpat, Bijnor, Moradabad, remained silent since morning in major markets, although shops remained open in mixed populated areas
 sadakon par logon kii awajahi rahi
 Most of the major markets, including Bhagat Singh Road, SD Market, Molahedi Bazaar, Dal Mandi in Muzaffarnagar city remained closed
 muslim bahulya ilaakon main dukaane khuli raheen
 In Meerut, BJP workers, led by state president Laxmikat Vajpayee, were seen urging traders to close shops
 bhaajapa ke band ko vyapaariyon kaa samarthan mila
 Locks were hanging all day in most markets
 bhaajapa ke pradesh pravaktaa vijay bahudar pathak ne kaha ki rajya sarkaar kii bhedbhaavpurn or ekatarfa karrwai ke virodh main ravivaar ko pashchimi uttar pradesh main shantipurna band kaa aahvaan kiya gaya tha
 Traders from various cities of western Uttar Pradesh, including Meerut, fully supported the BJP in the bandh
 band na keval abhootpurv rahaa, balki ise prabhavi jan samarthan mila
 He accused the Samajwadi Party (SP) government that in some districts including Bijnor, the police had taken the district heads into custody on Saturday
 aisi sthiti main bhi party dwaara aahut band puri tarah safal rahaa
 On the other hand, it was said from the administration that if BJP workers tried to forcibly close shops elsewhere, action would be taken against them, however, there were reports of forcible shops being closed by BJP workers in some places like Meerut, Noida, Saharanpur, Rampur
 tippaniyan It is noteworthy that the police arrested two BJP mlas - Sangeet Som and Suresh Rana - for the Muzaffarnagar violence
 pathak ne bataaya ki bhaajapa vidhayakon kii giraftaar or sapa sarkaar kii ekatarfa karrwai ke virodh main pradesh ke sabhi jila mukhyalayon par somvaar ko dharna-pradarshan hoga
